  1052. # [11:58] <AryehGregor> So does anyone have any ideas on how to define a MOZ_ENUM_CLASS that ensures the scoping semantics of enum class work in non-C++11 compilers?
  1053. # [11:59] <AryehGregor> "enum class Enum { A, B, C };" means that Enum is now a type, but A/B/C are accessible as Enum::A/Enum::B/Enum::C and not in the global scope.
